**PR number:** 33  
**Verdict:** `skipped` (lead-only merge gate — teammate does not run Codex)  
**LOC stats:** 1 file changed, +22 insertions, -4 deletions (`src/routes/item-form.tsx`)

**What was implemented:**
1. In edit mode, after loading the item, the parent folder is now loaded via `getFolderById(item.folderId)`.
2. If the parent folder is missing (`null`) or soft-deleted (`deletedAt !== null`), the same error UI used by create mode is rendered — the form is not shown.
3. Added the `retryToken` pattern (matching `folder.tsx`) so the Retry button re-fetches both the item and the parent folder.
4. Hydration in edit mode now gates on both `item` and `folder` being loaded, preventing a brief flash of the form before the folder check completes.

- `pnpm typecheck` — PASS
- `pnpm build` — PASS

**PR URL:** https://github.com/Benjamin-Sterrett/anwarallys-fabric-inventory/pull/33  
**PR number:** 33  
**Verdict:** `skipped` (lead-only merge gate — teammate does not run Codex)  
**LOC stats:** 1 file changed, +22 insertions, -4 deletions (`src/routes/item-form.tsx`)

**What was implemented:**
1. In edit mode, after loading the item, the parent folder is now loaded via `getFolderById(item.folderId)`.
2. If the parent folder is missing (`null`) or soft-deleted (`deletedAt !== null`), the same error UI used by create mode is rendered — the form is not shown.
3. Added the `retryToken` pattern (matching `folder.tsx`) so the Retry button re-fetches both the item and the parent folder.
4. Hydration in edit mode now gates on both `item` and `folder` being loaded, preventing a brief flash of the form before the folder check completes.

**Checks passed:**
- `pnpm typecheck` — PASS
- `pnpm build` — PASS

Final state: server-only reconcile reads, actor-scoped queries, two-outcome reconcile (`found | inconclusive`), inconclusive force-reload UX, ES5-safe UUID fallback for older Android WebViews, server-authoritative mount-time reads on `rolls-adjust.tsx`, time-bound replay defense REMOVED (it was broken — `serverTimestamp()` resolves to the same `request.time` for both `movement.at` and `item.updatedAt` in a successful tx, so the time-bound query still matched the previous movement). R9 self-replay finding deferred under `owner_override` to PRJ-892 (write-side idempotency is the proper defense; threat is null in the 2-3 person pilot scope).
- **PRJ-789** ✅ (PR #24, squash `a7dfa5e`) — Item-detail page at `/items/{itemId}`. Hosts the Adjust-stock entry, persistent Undo affordance (15-sec window anchored on server-stamped `Movement.at`, snapshot-consistency-gated, clock-skew-clamped), movement history list with Reversal badges and a truncation hint when >50 entries exist, and the Edit-metadata link. Item-row tap from folder browse now routes here (was `/edit`). Mount uses cache-backed read for offline-friendliness; safety comes from PRJ-890 server rules + server-stamped `Movement.at`. Clean APPROVE on round 3.

**One real bug surfaced and was root-caused (debug-workflow Quick path):** items/create rejected with `firestore/permission-denied` when the parent folder was a legacy prototype-era doc (`refuge`, lacking the v1 `ancestors` field). Folder reads passed because the read rule checks no shape, and `folderConverter.fromFirestore` silently coerces `d.ancestors ?? []` — masking the malformed shape from the UI. Items/create rule re-derives `folderAncestors` from the live folder doc and fails when `ancestors` is null. Root cause: the locked "no data migration — full replacement" decision was never executed before PRJ-886 deployed the rules. Fix was operational, not code: wiped legacy data with Shaaiz's explicit consent.

// Staff/admin user reads + writes (PRJ-856). All wrappers go through
// `getDb()` and return `Result<T>`. Init failures map to
// `firestore/no-db` / `firestore/init-failed`; operational failures
// preserve the SDK's `FirebaseError.code` (folders.ts/movements.ts pattern).
//
// `createStaffUser` provisioning model:
//   - TRANSIENT secondary Firebase app + Auth instance (inMemoryPersistence)
//     so `createUserWithEmailAndPassword` does NOT replace the admin's
//     primary session. `deleteApp` in `finally` prevents instance leaks.
//   - On Firestore-write failure, compensating-delete the just-created
//     Auth account ONLY when the Firestore error code is in
//     ROLLBACKABLE_FIRESTORE_CODES (definitive pre-write rejection).
//     Ambiguous codes (`unavailable`, `aborted`, etc.) could mean the
//     write IS persisted server-side; rolling back then would create the
//     inverse orphan (live /users doc, deleted Auth account).
//   - On ambiguous Auth-create rejection (network/timeout/internal/unknown),
//     surface "verify in Firebase Console" — the account may exist server
//     side and a blind retry would hit `auth/email-already-in-use`.
// Caller surfaces orphan paths to admin for Firebase Console reconciliation.

<!-- call_id: tool_KJi5zmmxB9PFDyWhxvG1dvRj -->
{
  "id": "d06baf64-a626-436f-ba82-5c611ddc4392",
  "title": "Server-authoritative mount-time reads on safety-critical routes (PRJ-883 follow-up)",
  "description": "## Context\n\nPRJ-883 (correlation-ID for atomic stock-write reconciliation, merged 2026-04-26) shipped with one Codex P2 finding deferred under `owner_override`: the timeout-recovery path on `rolls-adjust.tsx` instructs the operator to reload the page when the reconcile is inconclusive, but the route's mount logic uses cache-backed `getItemById()` rather than `getItemByIdFromServer()`. After a manual reload the new mount can repopulate from persistent local cache — especially if the device is offline or Firestore hasn't fully settled the original transaction — so the operator could still see stale on-hand state on the freshly-reloaded page.\n\nThis isn't unique to `rolls-adjust.tsx`. Several routes in the v1 SPA load critical state via cache-backed reads at mount: `item-form.tsx`, `folder.tsx`, `staff.tsx`, etc. The persistent local cache was enabled deliberately (offline-friendly browsing) but it creates a cache-vs-server-truth mismatch on safety-critical surfaces — most acutely on the stock-adjust route, where pre-commit transaction state can persist in cache for several seconds after the original write.\n\n`getItemByIdFromServer` already exists (PRJ-787 R5) for the post-write reconcile path. The pattern is sound. What's missing is using it on mount of safety-critical routes.\n\n## Requirements\n\n* Audit which routes load state that is safety-critical (stock-correctness or audit-attribution affecting). Initial list:\n  * `src/routes/rolls-adjust.tsx` — stock adjustment surface. **Highest priority.** Mount-time read of `RollItem` should be server-authoritative.\n  * `src/routes/item-form.tsx` (edit mode) — editing item metadata. Cache reads here are probably fine; folder/sku changes don't affect stock correctness.\n  * `src/routes/folder.tsx` — browse + counts. Cache is fine.\n  * `src/routes/staff.tsx` — admin operations on staff. Cache is risky here too: a stale cache could let an admin attempt to deactivate a user who's already been deactivated by a concurrent admin in another session, with confusing error states.\n* For each safety-critical route, replace mount-time `getItemById()`/etc with `getItemByIdFromServer()`/etc. Existing `getItemByIdFromServer` pattern (in `src/lib/queries/items.ts`) is the template — caller MUST handle `firestore/unavailable`, no cache fallback by design.\n* For non-safety-critical routes, keep cache-backed reads (offline-friendly UX is the explicit pilot policy).\n* Add a doc comment at each safety-critical route's mount-effect explaining why server-only is required there.\n\n## Acceptance Criteria\n\n* `rolls-adjust.tsx` mount uses `getItemByIdFromServer()` instead of `getItemById()`. Manual reload on the inconclusive recovery path now guarantees a fresh server snapshot of `remainingMeters`.\n* `staff.tsx` mount uses server-authoritative reads for `listActiveStaff`/`listInactiveStaff` (or equivalent helpers added that bypass cache).\n* Other routes audited and either kept on cache (with a comment explaining why) or moved to server (with a comment explaining why).\n* `firestore/unavailable` (offline at mount-time) surfaces a clear \"you appear to be offline; this page needs a server connection\" message — does NOT silent-fall-back to cache.\n* No regression in offline browsing of folder tree (`folder.tsx` stays cache-friendly).\n\n## Affected Files/Components\n\n* `src/lib/queries/items.ts` — likely already has `getItemByIdFromServer` (verify).\n* `src/lib/queries/users.ts` — may need to add `listActiveStaffFromServer` / `listInactiveStaffFromServer` helpers.\n* `src/routes/rolls-adjust.tsx` — primary fix.\n* `src/routes/staff.tsx` — secondary.\n* Other routes: audit and document decision.\n\n## Dependencies\n\n* None blocking. Should ship before pilot if the inconclusive-recovery flow on `rolls-adjust.tsx` is to be operator-trustworthy under offline conditions.\n\n## Technical Notes\n\n* Vite + persistent local cache means mount-time reads are extra suspect on tablets that move in/out of Wi-Fi range. The pilot environment (storeroom) has documented unreliable Wi-Fi.\n* `getItemByIdFromServer()` requires the SDK to round-trip; if offline, it errors with `firestore/unavailable`. Routes need to handle this error visibly (per the project's \"never silent fail\" invariant).\n* Could be implemented as a smaller scoped change: ONLY `rolls-adjust.tsx` first (the route that prompted this ticket). Other routes' cache-vs-server tradeoff can be evaluated separately if they're not safety-critical.\n* Recommend Path A (`rolls-adjust.tsx` only) for v1 pilot. Wider audit can happen as a follow-up after pilot data shows whether the cache-staleness pattern bites in practice.",
  "url": "https://linear.app/vmps/issue/PRJ-893/server-authoritative-mount-time-reads-on-safety-critical-routes-prj"
}

{
  "description": "PRJ-880 teammate implementation",
  "prompt": "You are an autonomous implementer on an agent team. Run the full dev-workflow Fast path straight through — Codex replaces human at all gates. Do NOT stop or wait for approval. Complete all steps and create the PR.\n\n**Scope includes ALL implementation work:** code changes, skill file updates, documentation edits, and AGENTS.md modifications. If the ticket touches any of these, implement them fully — do not defer to the lead.\n\nTicket: PRJ-880 — Items list paging in folder browse (cursor-based, default 50/page) | Worktree: /tmp/dev-workflow-worktrees/20260426/PRJ-880\n\n## Context\n\nPRJ-879 added a live `onSnapshot` subscription for items in folder browse. The list now updates live but has no paging — all items in a folder render at once. For folders with large inventories this could be unwieldy.\n\n## Requirements\n\n* Add cursor-based paging to the items list in `src/routes/folder.tsx`.\n* Default page size: 50 items.\n* Use Firestore `startAfter` + `limit` cursor pattern (not offset-based — Firestore doesn't support efficient offset queries).\n* The existing `subscribeToActiveItemsInFolder` (PRJ-879) uses `onSnapshot` for live updates. Paging with `onSnapshot` is more complex because the SDK's `Query` object is immutable. Consider:\n  * **Option A:** Keep the live subscription but page client-side (slice the subscribed array). Simplest, still gets live updates, but all docs are held in memory.\n  * **Option B:** Replace the subscription with a one-shot `getDocs` + cursor for paging, add a manual \"Refresh\" button. Loses live updates but scales better.\n  * **Option C:** Hybrid — subscribe to a limited query (first page) and show a \"Load more\" that fetches subsequent pages one-shot. Most complex.\n* **Recommended:** Option A (client-side paging) for v1 pilot. The pilot has 2-3 staff and <500 items total; client-side paging is sufficient and preserves the live-update UX from PRJ-879.\n* Add \"Previous\" / \"Next\" buttons below the items list. If Semgrep or security review rejects after 1 fix → exit with blocked status.\n\n### Phase 3: Deliver + PR (DELIVER → PR creation + lead-only review)\n- Read dw-deliver skill at ~/.claude/skills/dw-deliver/SKILL.md and follow it — commit + push\n- Create PR with `gh pr create`\n- **Persist PR number immediately after `gh pr create`:**\n  ```bash\n  STATE_FILE=\"$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)/.dw-state.json\"\n  PR_NUM=$(gh pr list --head \"$(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD)\" --json number --jq '.[0].number')\n  _TFS=$(mktemp \"$(dirname \"$STATE_FILE\")/.dw-state.XXXXXX\")\n  jq --arg pr \"$PR_NUM\" '.durable_ids.pr_number = ($pr | tonumber)' \"$STATE_FILE\" > \"$_TFS\" && mv -f \"$_TFS\" \"$STATE_FILE\"\n  ```\n- Write skip decision entry with reviewer_role: \"teammate\":\n  ```bash\n  STATE_FILE=\"$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)/.dw-state.json\"\n  HEAD_SHA=$(git rev-parse HEAD 2>/dev/null)\n  _TS=$(date -u +%FT%TZ)\n  DECISION=$(jq -nc --arg sha \"$HEAD_SHA\" --arg ts \"$_TS\" \\\n    '{step:\"pr-review\",reviewer_role:\"teammate\",gate:\"skipped\",head_sha:$sha,timestamp:$ts,reason:\"lead-only merge gate — teammate does not run Codex\"}')\n  _TFS=$(mktemp \"$(dirname \"$STATE_FILE\")/.dw-state.XXXXXX\")\n  jq --argjson d \"$DECISION\" --arg ts \"$_TS\" '\n    .decisions += [$d] |\n    .phases[\"pr-review\"] = {\"status\": \"skipped\", \"completed_at\": $ts} |\n    .current_phase = \"pr-review\" |\n    .last_updated = $ts\n  ' \"$STATE_FILE\" > \"$_TFS\" && mv -f \"$_TFS\" \"$STATE_FILE\" || { rm -f \"$_TFS\"; exit 1; }\n  ```\n- Validate state file integrity:\n  ```bash\n  _WT_ROOT=\"$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)\"\n  bash ~/.claude/scripts/validate-state-file.sh \"$_WT_ROOT/.dw-state.json\"\n  ```\n- Touch `.agent-done` at completion\n\nOutput at completion: PR URL, PR number, verdict: \"skipped\" (lead-only gate), LOC stats.\nDo NOT merge. `gh pr merge` is FORBIDDEN from teammate context.\nDo NOT invoke dw-pr-review. }
